You can view the detailed information of the action including the type of events, date/time of occurrence, and a brief description. \r\n\r\nPerform multiple transfers\r\nWhenever you want to transfer multiple files, a queue becomes necessary. Transfer queue maintains the list of files and folders which are ready for transfer, currently transferring or failed to transfer.
